# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 02:32:16.806321

### Base Program

```py
def common_factors(a: int, b: int) -> int:
    from math import gcd

    g = gcd(a, b)
    count = 0
    for i in range(1, int(g**0.5) + 1):
        if g % i == 0:
            count += 1
            if i * i != g:
                count += 1
    return count
```

### Input

```json
[30, 89]
```

</details>

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def common_factors(a: int, b: int) -> int:
    from math import gcd
    g = gcd(a, b)
    count = 0
    for i in range(1, int(g ** 0.5) + 1):
        if g % i == 0:
            count += 1
            if i * i != g:
                count += 1
    return count
```

</details>

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def common_factors(var_0: int, var_1: int) -> int:
    from math import gcd
    g = gcd(var_0, var_1)
    count = 0
    for i in range(1, int(g ** 0.5) + 1):
        if g % i == 0:
            count += 1
            if i * i != g:
                count += 1
    return count
```

</details>

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def common_factors(a: int, b: int) -> int:
    from math import gcd
    g = gcd(a, b)
    count = 0
    for i in range(1, 1 + int(g ** 0.5)):
        if g % i == 0:
            count += 1
            if i * i != g:
                count += 1
    return count
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def common_factors(var_2: int, var_3: int) -> int:
    from math import gcd
    g = gcd(var_2, var_3)
    count = 0
    for i in range(1, 1 + int(g ** 0.5)):
        if g % i == 0:
            count += 1
            if i * i != g:
                count += 1
    return count
```
